################### MEM Science Convention ######################
### More Events Mod
###
### The Science Convention
### Original Idea by PossessedLemon
### Script by binaryferret. <Twitter: @binaryferret>
### Writing by Briv
###
###
### In order to bloat prevent in the main file (mem_sciencecon_events.txt)
### All the critical success events were moved into this file. 
###
### The reason: On Critical success in science convention events you
### are rewarded with a tech that is available to you having a large
### amount of progress added to it. 
###
### Unfortunetly the scripting language currently doesn't provide a 
### way to say 'Out of the techs I'm currently researching, choose a
### random one, and apply progress'
###
### In order to do this, and provide a bit of a random nature to it
### I had to bring in every TECH into the code and do checks on it.
###
### I added a bit of a random nature to it, as before that you'd be
### always get the top most tech available to you. 
###
### Hoping in the future they will bring in more research focused
### effects/conditions that can be called then this can be shrank!
###
#################################################################

namespace = mem_sciencecon_event

#Reward for a success
@mem_sciencecon_reward_1 = 150 #on your own
@mem_sciencecon_reward_2 = 175 #1 or more
@mem_sciencecon_reward_3 = 200 #3 or more
@mem_sciencecon_reward_4 = 250 #6 or more

################### mem_sciencecon_event.91 ######################
### Engineering Techs
###
### If selected from the random list in event.3 then this will
### provide some randomness to selecting which tech you will
### gain progress too from the available options available to you
##################################################################
country_event = { 
  id = mem_sciencecon_event.91
  hide_window = yes
  is_triggered_only = yes

  immediate = {  

    random_list = {
      34 = { 
        set_variable = {
          which = mem_sciencecon_rnd
          value = 1
        }
      }
      33 = {
        set_variable = {
          which = mem_sciencecon_rnd
          value = 2
        }
      }
      33 = {
        set_variable = {
          which = mem_sciencecon_rnd
          value = 3
        }
      }

    if = {
      limit = {
        has_tech_option = tech_spaceport_1
        check_variable = {
          which = mem_sciencecon_rnd
          value = 1
        }

      break = yes

        if = {
          limit = {
            has_tech_option = tech_spaceport_1

            value = -1

        if = {
          limit = {
            has_tech_option = tech_mine_satramene
          }
          change_variable = {
            which = mem_sciencecon_rnd
            value = -1
          }
        }
      }
    }
    if = {
      limit = {
        has_tech_option = tech_mine_dark_matter
        check_variable = {
          which = mem_sciencecon_rnd
          value = 1
        }
      }
      country_event = { id = mem_sciencecon_event.380 days = 1}
      break = yes
      else = {
        if = {
          limit = {
            has_tech_option = tech_mine_dark_matter
          }
          change_variable = {
            which = mem_sciencecon_rnd
            value = -1
          }
        }
      }
    }
    ##If somehow we have fallen through at least reward the player with something.
    country_event = {id = mem_sciencecon_event.4 days = 1 }
  }
}

  title = "mem_sciencecon.3.name"
  desc = {
    text = mem_sciencecon.3.desc
    trigger = {
      has_country_flag = mem_sciencecon_host
      NOT = {        
        has_country_flag = mem_sciencecon_someone_accepted
      }
    }
  }
  desc = {
    text = mem_sciencecon.3.a.desc
    trigger = {
      has_country_flag = mem_sciencecon_host
      has_country_flag = mem_sciencecon_someone_accepted
    }
  }
  desc = {
    text = mem_sciencecon.3.b.desc
    trigger = {
      NOT = {
        has_country_flag = mem_sciencecon_host
      }
    }
  }
  picture = GFX_evt_hangar_bay
  show_sound = event_default
  is_triggered_only = yes

  option = {
    name = mem_sciencecon.3.a
    add_physics_research = @mem_sciencecon_reward_1
    add_society_research = @mem_sciencecon_reward_1
    add_engineering_research = @mem_sciencecon_reward_1
    add_tech_progress = {
      tech = tech_engos_vapor
      progress = 0.8
    }
  }
}
